# Public Theorem Index ‚ÄĒ GraphCanonizationProofs

Index of public Lean theorems, lemmas, and definitions in the GraphCanonizationProofs project (active source), grouped by source file path. Archived counterparts live in `Archive/PublicTheoremIndex.md`. Private declarations live in `PrivateTheoremIndex.md`.

Maintained by `scripts/GenerateTheoremIndexes.py rewrite --with-line-numbers`: the **Name**, **Line**, and **Notes** columns are computed from source; **Description** is hand-written and preserved. Prose between tables (this note, the Legend, `### ‚Ä¶` sub-headers, per-file descriptions) is passed through untouched.
## Legend

- **Line**: Source-line range `start-end` covering the declaration's header (attached doc comment / attributes) and its full body. Collapses to a single number when the declaration occupies one line. Gaps between theorems represent whitespace or comments.
- **Description**: What the declaration achieves / why a consumer would use it (not how it is proved), in ‚Č§ 2 sentences. A leading `¬ß‚Ä¶` section marker or **bold anchor** links it to the documentation.
- **Notes**: Computed from source ‚ÄĒ the infrastructure kind (`Definition`/`Structure`/`Inductive`/`Class`/`abbrev`/`axiom`/`Instance`), `noncomputable`, and `@[‚Ä¶]` attributes. `private` is omitted (it is encoded by the public/private index split).

## ChainDescent.lean

| Name | Line | Description | Notes |
|------|------|-------------|-------|
| `POE` | 76-80 | Partial-order entries: the three values `less`, `unknown`, `greater` that populate a `PMatrix`. | Inductive |
| `neg` | 93-97 | Antisymmetric reverse on one entry: swaps `less`/`greater`, fixes `unknown`. | Definition |
| `neg_neg` | 99-100 | `neg` is an involution: `neg (neg e) = e`. | `@[simp]` |
| `POE.swap` | 102-105 | ŌÉ-swap on one entry (the matrix-wide relabelling of the direction-symmetry argument); coincides with `neg`. | Definition |
| `POE.swap_swap` | 107 | ŌÉ-swap is an involution: `swap (swap e) = e`. | `@[simp]` |
| `swap_less` | 109 | `swap .less = .greater`. | `@[simp]` |
| `swap_greater` | 110 | `swap .greater = .less`. | `@[simp]` |
| `swap_unknown` | 111 | `swap .unknown = .unknown`. | `@[simp]` |
| `PMatrix` | 117-118 | The partial-order matrix type `Fin n ‚Üí Fin n ‚Üí POE`. | Definition |
| `swap` | 124-125 | Pointwise ŌÉ-swap of a `PMatrix`: swap `less` with `greater` at every entry. | Definition |
| `swap_swap` | 127-128 | ŌÉ-swap is an involution on `PMatrix`: `swap (swap P) = P`. | `@[simp]` |
| `Antisymmetric` | 130-132 | A `PMatrix` is antisymmetric when `P i j = POE.neg (P j i)` for all `i, j`. | Definition |
| `AdjMatrix` | 141-142 | Self-contained adjacency matrix on `Fin n`, wrapping a `Fin n ‚Üí Fin n ‚Üí Nat` field. | Structure |
| `applyGuess` | 146-153 | Apply a single guess `(a, b, dir)` to `P`: set `P a b := dir`, `P b a := neg dir`, leaving every other entry unchanged. Does not transitively close. | Definition |
| `closeStep` | 180-193 | Single-step transitive closure: derive `P i j` from a uniform chain `i ‚Üí k ‚Üí j`, with `less`-chains taking priority over `greater`-chains at ties. | Definition |
| `transitiveClose` | 195-199 | Transitive closure of a `PMatrix` by iterating `closeStep` `n*n` times ‚ÄĒ enough rounds to reach fixpoint. | Definition |
| `conflictMatrix` | 230-243 | Concrete 4-vertex witness with a conflicted pair `(0,1)` carrying both a `less`-chain and a `greater`-chain; refutes ŌÉ-swap commutation. | Definition |
| `closeStep_swap_false` | 262-271 | **Refutation:** `closeStep` does not commute with ŌÉ-swap unconditionally ‚ÄĒ the `less`-first tie-break is not ŌÉ-symmetric (fails on `conflictMatrix`). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `transitiveClose_swap_false` | 292-306 | **Refutation:** `transitiveClose` does not commute with ŌÉ-swap unconditionally (witnessed by `conflictMatrix`). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `Colouring` | 310-311 | A vertex colouring `Fin n ‚Üí Nat`. | Definition |
| `signature` | 313-319 | Multiset signature of vertex `v` under colouring `Ōá` and state `(adj, P)`: the `(Ōá u, adj.adj v u, P v u)` tuples over all `u ‚Č† v`. | Definition |
| `POE.toNat` | 321-326 | Numeric code for a `POE` entry matching the C# packing: `less ‚Ü¶ 0`, `unknown ‚Ü¶ 1`, `greater ‚Ü¶ 2`. | Definition |
| `encTuple` | 332-338 | Canonical injection of a signature tuple `(colour, edge-label, POE)` into `Nat` (Cantor pairing); mirrors the C# neighbour-tuple packing. | Definition |
| `sigKey` | 347-354 | Canonical refinement key of a vertex: its old colour followed by the sorted encoded signature multiset (the C# `[own-colour, sorted neighbour-tuples]`). | Definition |
| `sigKey_eq_iff` | 356-370 | Two vertices share a `sigKey` iff they have the same old colour and the same signature. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `warmRefine` | 399-409 | Warm 1-WL refinement: iterate `refineStep` `n` times from `initial`; concrete and computable. | Definition |
| `refineStep` / `refineStep_iff` | ~320-417 | **Concrete (2026-05-30, no longer axioms):** `refineStep adj P Ōá v := Encodable.encode (sigKey adj P Ōá v)` (own colour + sorted encoded signature = the C# `WarmPartition.RefineRound`); `refineStep_iff` (same colour ‚üļ same old colour + same signature) is now a **theorem**. Removes `refineStep`/`refineStep_iff` from the axiom basis project-wide. Helpers: `POE.toNat`(_injective), `encTuple`(_injective), `sigKey`, `sigKey_eq_iff`. | Def + theorem |
| `samePartition` | 413-416 | Two colourings induce the same partition: `Ōá‚āĀ i = Ōá‚āĀ j ‚ÜĒ Ōá‚āā i = Ōá‚āā j` for every `i, j`. | Definition |
| `samePartition.refl` | 422 | `samePartition` is reflexive. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `samePartition.symm` | 424-425 | `samePartition` is symmetric. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `samePartition.trans` | 427-429 | `samePartition` is transitive. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `refineStep_refines` | 435-440 | **Refinement is split-only (one round).** Equal refined colour implies equal old colour. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `warmRefine_refines` | 442-468 | Warm refinement is split-only: equal warm-refined colour implies equal starting colour. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `cell_split_uniform_false` | 571-596 | **Refutation:** cell-mates do not in general keep equal signatures after a guess plus TC (witnessed by `witnessP0`, the gap fixed only by singleton-cell `a`, `b`). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `iterate_refineStep_preserves_singleton` | 627-640 | Iterating refinement preserves a singleton for any number of rounds. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `signature_eq_of_samePartition` | 658-685 | **Signature equality is a partition invariant of the colouring:** partition-equal colourings induce the same signature-equality relation between vertices. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `warm_6_2` | 687-764 | **¬ß6.2 direction invariance.** With `a, b` `ŌáőĻ`-singletons, warm refinement after `a < b` and after `b < a` induce the same partition. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `warmRefine_swap` | 780-822 | **Direction-blindness (Q1).** Warm refinement on `P` and on its ŌÉ-swap induce the same partition. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `applyGuess_comm` | 836-854 | **Q2 ‚ÄĒ guesses commute.** Guessing on `{a,b}` then `{b,c}` (pairwise-distinct vertices) gives the same `(adj, P)` as the reverse order, since the writes touch disjoint matrix entries. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `warmRefine_agree_off'` | 875-922 | **¬ß6.2 ‚ÄĒ composable cross-branch sharing.** Matrices agreeing off `D` and `samePartition`-equal starting colourings (with `D` all `Ōá`-singletons) yield the same warm-refined partition; the cross-level form that chains across descent levels. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `warmRefine_agree_off` | 924-958 | **¬ß6.2 ‚ÄĒ the cell partition depends only on the matrix off the decision set `D`.** Matrices agreeing off `D` (its vertices `ŌáőĻ`-singletoned) yield the same partition; the same-`ŌáőĻ` specialisation of `warmRefine_agree_off'`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `PartitionInvariant` | 975-979 | A target-cell selector is partition-invariant when it depends only on the partition a colouring induces, not on raw colour values. | Definition |
| `target_direction_blind` | 981-990 | **¬ß6.2 spine ‚ÄĒ base case.** For a partition-invariant selector, the target cell chosen after `a < b` equals the one after `b < a`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `target_agree_off` | 992-1005 | **¬ß6.2 spine ‚ÄĒ inductive step.** For a partition-invariant selector and matrices agreeing off a singletoned decision set `D`, the target cell is the same even when the start colourings only agree up to partition. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `Egnd` | 1034-1035 | **¬ß13.** The canonical ground set on `Fin n`: ordered pairs `(i, j)` with `i < j`. | Definition |
| `Pof` | 1043-1056 | **¬ß13.** Commit a set `S ‚äÜ Egnd n` of pair-guesses into a P-matrix: write `less` at `(u,v) ‚ąą S`, `greater` at `(v,u)`, leaving other entries unchanged. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `cl` | 1058-1063 | **¬ß13.** Propagation closure on pair-guesses: the canonical pairs whose endpoints get separated by warm refinement after committing `S`. | Definition |
| `SingletonAt` | 1073-1075 | The fresh-colour hypothesis at a pair `p`: both `p.1` and `p.2` are `ŌáőĻ`-singletons. | Definition |
| `cl_extensive` | 1077-1092 | **¬ß13 M1 ‚ÄĒ extensiveness of `cl`.** For canonical `S` whose vertices are all `ŌáőĻ`-singletons, every pair in `S` lies in `cl S`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `FullyDiscrete` | 1158-1160 | A colouring is fully discrete when every vertex is its own `ŌáőĻ`-singleton. | Definition |
| `cl_monotone_discrete` | 1162-1179 | **¬ß13 M0, vacuous case.** Under `FullyDiscrete`, every canonical pair lies in every `cl S`, so `cl S = Egnd n` and monotonicity carries no structural information. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `TVerticesSingletons` | 1192-1194 | Every endpoint of every pair in `T` is a `ŌáőĻ`-singleton. | Definition |
| `warmRefine_samePartition_T_individualised` | 1196-1281 | **¬ß13 M0, strong form.** Warm refinement under `Pof P‚āÄ S` and `Pof P‚āÄ T` induces the *same* partition when `S ‚äÜ T` and every endpoint of every `T`-pair is a `ŌáőĻ`-singleton. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `cl_monotone_T_individualised` | 1283-1294 | **¬ß13 M0 ‚ÄĒ monotonicity of `cl`** under the T-individualised hypothesis: `S ‚äÜ T` implies `cl S ‚äÜ cl T`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `cl_idempotent` | 1320-1334 | **¬ß13 M2 ‚ÄĒ idempotence of `cl`** under fresh-colour individualisation of `S ‚ą™ cl S`: `cl (cl S) = cl S`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `Pof_fs` | 1406-1412 | **¬ß14.** Finset-based computable analogue of `Pof`, enabling `decide`-checkable refutations. | Definition |
| `commitsToP` | 1414-1416 | **¬ß14.** All-unknown-base commits-to-matrix shortcut: `Pof_fs (fun _ _ => .unknown) S`. | Definition |
| `cl_prov` | 1418-1423 | **¬ß14.** Provenance closure (TC-based): the canonical pair-guesses whose direction is decided by `transitiveClose` of `commitsToP S`. | Definition |
| `cl_prov_empty` | 1454-1463 | **¬ß14 CL0 for `cl_prov`:** `cl_prov ‚ąÖ = ‚ąÖ`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `cl_prov_extensive` | 1465-1479 | **¬ß14 CL1 for `cl_prov`:** for canonical `S`, every commit's direct `less` write survives transitive closure, so `S ‚äÜ cl_prov S`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `cl_prov_M3_false` | 1497-1507 | **¬ß14 ‚ÄĒ refutes matroid M3 exchange for `cl_prov`.** A concrete `n=5, S={(1,2),(3,4)}, x=(2,3), y=(1,4)` counterexample where the M3 premise holds but the conclusion fails; machine-checked by `decide`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `hasLessChain` | 1521-1524 | Existence of a `.less`-chain in `P` from `i` to `j` via some intermediate `k` with both edges `.less`. | Definition |
| `hasGreaterChain` | 1526-1528 | Existence of a `.greater`-chain in `P` from `i` to `j` via some intermediate `k`. | Definition |
| `CanConsistent` | 1530-1534 | A `PMatrix` is canonical-consistent when every `.less` entry sits at `i.val < j.val` and every `.greater` entry at `i.val > j.val`. | Definition |
| `LessMono` | 1536-1539 | One-sided `.less`-direction entry-wise monotonicity between two matrices: `P i j = .less ‚Üí Q i j = .less`. | Definition |
| `cl_prov_monotone` | 1809-1834 | **¬ß14 CL3 ‚ÄĒ monotonicity for `cl_prov`:** canonical `S ‚äÜ T` implies `cl_prov S ‚äÜ cl_prov T`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `numUnknown` | 1843-1846 | Number of `.unknown` entries in a `PMatrix` ‚ÄĒ the strictly-decreasing potential bounding TC iteration. | Definition |
| `transitiveClose_idempotent` | 1974-1980 | **TC idempotence.** `transitiveClose (transitiveClose M) = transitiveClose M`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `cl_prov_idempotent` | 2011-2041 | **CL2 ‚ÄĒ idempotence.** `cl_prov (cl_prov S) = cl_prov S` for canonical `S`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `IndivStep` | 2128-2152 | Existential witness of one descent-step individualisation: a colouring `Ōá'` that singletons every vertex in target `T` and refines `Ōá` outside `T`. Data, not a function ‚ÄĒ the trace carries one per step. | Structure |
| `singletons_union` | 2156-2177 | **D-singletons preserved.** If `Ōá` singletons every `v ‚ąą D`, an `IndivStep` with target `T` singletons every `v ‚ąą D ‚ą™ T`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `IndivStep.default` | 2211-2262 | **Concrete `IndivStep` witness.** A constructive individualisation step (parity-tagged base-`n` encoding), proving traces exist at every level so the spine theorem is non-vacuous. | Definition |
| `DescentTrace` | 2271-2309 | Inductive predicate: `(D, P, ŌáőĻ)` is reachable by `k` descent steps from `(P‚āÄ, ŌáőĻ‚āÄ)` under selector `sel`, each step carrying an `IndivStep` witness and a matrix agreeing with `P‚āÄ` off the enlarged decision set. | Inductive |
| `singletons` | 2313-2330 | **Trace invariant.** A trace's colouring singletons its whole decision set `D`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `P_agrees` | 2332-2342 | **Trace invariant.** A trace's matrix agrees with `P‚āÄ` on every entry with an endpoint outside `D`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `SpineChain` | 2346-2354 | Bundle of a `DescentTrace` with its derived state `(D, P, ŌáőĻ)`. The spine theorem is branch-independence of two such chains. | Structure |
| `partition` | 2361-2365 | The chain's level-`k` partition: warm refinement of its accumulated `(P, ŌáőĻ)`. | Definition |
| `spine_branch_independent` | 2386-2460 | **The spine theorem (branch independence).** Any two `DescentTrace`s through `k` levels agree on the accumulated `D` (literal) and the level-`k` partition (`samePartition`) ‚ÄĒ handing the oracle one fixed partition instead of `2^d` refinement worlds. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `SpineChain.branch_independent` | 2462-2471 | **The spine theorem, `SpineChain` wrapper.** Two chains at level `k` share `D` and level-`k` partition. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `defaultColouring` | 2492-2502 | The level-`k` colouring of the default reference chain: iterate refine-then-individualise (via `IndivStep.default`) from `ŌáőĻ‚āÄ`, with the matrix held fixed at `P‚āÄ`. | Definition |
| `defaultD` | 2504-2513 | The level-`k` decision set of the default chain: accumulate `sel (warmRefine adj P‚āÄ (defaultColouring k))` across all levels. | Definition |
| `defaultTrace` | 2515-2528 | The concrete `DescentTrace` realising the default construction, using `IndivStep.default` at every level and `P = P‚āÄ` throughout. | Definition |
| `defaultSpineChain` | 2530-2538 | The concrete reference `SpineChain` at every level, bundling `defaultD`/`P‚āÄ`/`defaultColouring`/`defaultTrace`. | Definition |
| `SpineChain.eq_default` | 2540-2551 | **Reference corollary.** Every `SpineChain` at level `k` shares `D` and level-`k` partition with `defaultSpineChain` ‚ÄĒ there is a canonical level-`k` partition, computable by one deterministic descent. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `Discrete` | 2575-2578 | A colouring is discrete when every cell is a singleton ‚ÄĒ equivalently, `Ōá : Fin n ‚Üí Nat` is injective. | Definition |
| `of_samePartition` | 2582-2586 | Discreteness is `samePartition`-invariant: equal partitions transport `Discrete`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `SpineChain.IsLeaf` | 2601-2607 | A `SpineChain` reaches a leaf when its level-`k` partition is discrete (every vertex a singleton). | Definition |
| `TargetsNonsingletonCell` | 2622-2628 | Selector hypothesis: every returned vertex has a same-colour partner (`sel` only picks from non-singleton cells). | Definition |
| `NonemptyOnNonDiscrete` | 2630-2635 | Selector hypothesis: `sel Ōá` is non-empty whenever `Ōá` is not yet discrete. | Definition |
| `defaultD_univ_isLeaf` | 2637-2652 | **`D` covers all vertices ‚áí leaf.** When the accumulated decision set is the full vertex set, the default chain's spine partition is discrete. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `defaultD_grows_if_not_leaf` | 2654-2693 | **`D` strictly grows on every non-leaf step.** Under the two selector hypotheses, a non-leaf level-`k` chain has `|defaultD k| < |defaultD (k+1)|`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `defaultSpineChain_reaches_leaf` | 2695-2734 | **Leaf existence.** Under `TargetsNonsingletonCell` and `NonemptyOnNonDiscrete`, the default descent reaches a leaf within `n` levels. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `DirAssignment` | 2757-2763 | Order assignment relative to `(P‚āÄ, D)`: an antisymmetric matrix agreeing with `P‚āÄ` on every entry with an endpoint outside `D`. The linear oracle's input shape ‚ÄĒ a point in the order-label residual. | Structure |
| `default` | 2769-2776 | **Trivial `DirAssignment`.** When `P‚āÄ` is antisymmetric, `P‚āÄ` itself is a valid order assignment for any `D` (witnesses non-emptiness). | Definition |
| `samePartition_pair` | 2778-2790 | Any two `DirAssignment`s over the same `(P‚āÄ, D)`, refined against a `D`-singletoning colouring, induce the same partition. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `samePartition_chain` | 2792-2805 | **Spine equivalence.** A `DirAssignment` over a chain's `D`, refined against the chain's colouring, induces the chain's partition ‚ÄĒ the residual is exactly the choice of `DirAssignment`, partition fixed. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `flipPair` | 2809-2853 | **Single-pair direction flip.** Negate the `(a, b)` and `(b, a)` entries of a `DirAssignment` via `POE.neg`. The generator of the `Z‚āā` group action on direction choices. | Definition |
| `flipPair_idempotent` | 2867-2876 | **Flip is an involution.** Two applications of `flipPair` to the same pair return the original `DirAssignment` ‚ÄĒ the `Z‚āā` generator squares to identity. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `flipPair_partition_invariant` | 2878-2888 | **Flipping preserves the partition.** `ŌÉ` and `ŌÉ.flipPair a b` share the spine partition ‚ÄĒ the order labels move, the partition doesn't. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `flipPair_comm` | 2890-2914 | **Flips on disjoint pairs commute** ‚ÄĒ the abelian-ness of the `Z‚āā^d` action: distinct decisions don't interfere. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `IsAut` | 2942-2945 | A `Fin n`-permutation `ŌÄ` is a graph automorphism of `adj` when it preserves adjacency edge-by-edge: `adj.adj (ŌÄ v) (ŌÄ w) = adj.adj v w`. | Definition |
| `IsAut.refl` | 2951-2952 | The identity permutation is an automorphism. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `IsAut.trans` | 2954-2959 | Composition of automorphisms is an automorphism. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `IsAut.symm` | 2961-2967 | The inverse of an automorphism is an automorphism. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `labelledAdj` | 2971-2977 | **Labelled adjacency.** Adjacency matrix relabelled by `ŌÄ`: entry `(i, j)` is the original adjacency between `ŌÄ‚ĀĽ¬Ļ i` and `ŌÄ‚ĀĽ¬Ļ j`. | Definition |
| `labelledAdj_eq_of_isAut` | 2979-2992 | **Automorphisms fix the labelled adjacency.** `IsAut ŌÄ adj` implies `labelledAdj ŌÄ adj = adj.adj` ‚ÄĒ an automorphism is invisible at the labelled level. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `isAut_of_labelledAdj_eq` | 2994-3004 | **Converse.** A permutation preserving the labelled adjacency is an automorphism. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `vertexRankNat` | 3017-3019 | Strict rank of vertex `v`: the count of vertices `u` with `Ōá u < Ōá v`. | Definition |
| `vertexRank` | 3037-3039 | Vertex rank packaged as `Fin n` via `vertexRankNat_lt_n`. | Definition |
| `rankPerm` | 3079-3083 | **The rank permutation.** Bijection `Fin n ‚ČÉ Fin n` mapping each vertex to its colour-rank on a `Discrete` colouring. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `rankPerm_apply` | 3085-3086 | Unfolding lemma: `rankPerm Ōá h v = vertexRank Ōá v`. | `@[simp]` |
| `vertexRank_comp` | 3090-3109 | `vertexRank (Ōá ‚ąė g) v = vertexRank Ōá (g v)` ‚ÄĒ a pure `Finset.card` reindex along `g`. *(Relocated from `LinearOracle.lean` for the cascade oracle's `colourMatchPerm` (M-B).)* | ‚ÄĒ |
| `rankPerm_comp` | 3111-3131 | **Rank reindexing.** `rankPerm (Ōá ‚ąė e) = rankPerm Ōá ¬∑ e` ‚ÄĒ relabelling conjugate-shifts the rank permutation (the ¬ßL.5 conjugation gap). *(Relocated from `LinearOracle.lean`.)* | ‚ÄĒ |
| `SpineChain.canonAdj` | 3147-3173 | **Leaf canonical adjacency.** Given a leaf `SpineChain` and a `DirAssignment ŌÉ` over its `D`, relabel `adj` by the rank permutation of the warm-refined partition. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `matrixLT` | 3177-3184 | **Row-major lex strict less-than on `n √ó n` matrices.** The first disagreeing cell `(i, j)` (row-then-column order) has `M‚āĀ i j < M‚āā i j`. | Definition |
| `PMatrix.fintype` | 3216-3221 | `Fintype` instance for `PMatrix n`, stated explicitly since `PMatrix` is a `def` and so does not inherit the `Pi` instance transparently. | Instance |
| `DirAssignment.fintype` | 3227-3237 | **`Fintype` on `DirAssignment P‚āÄ D`.** Obtained by injecting the ŌÉ-field into the `Fintype` `PMatrix n`. | Instance, `noncomputable` |
| `relabelMatrix` | 3241-3248 | **Relabel a bare matrix** `Fin n ‚Üí Fin n ‚Üí Nat` by a permutation `ŌÄ`: entry `(i,j)` becomes `M (ŌÄ‚ĀĽ¬Ļ i) (ŌÄ‚ĀĽ¬Ļ j)`. Lets `LeafTwistSpec` state the leaf-relabelling property without re-wrapping as an `AdjMatrix`. | Definition |
| `MatrixLex` | 3250-3255 | `Fin n ‚Üí Fin n ‚Üí Nat` viewed under the row-major lex order via nested `Pi.Lex`. | `abbrev` |
| `toMatrixLex` | 3257-3260 | Wrap a matrix into its Lex'd form (identity at runtime ‚ÄĒ `Lex` is a type synonym). | Definition |
| `ofMatrixLex` | 3262-3264 | Unwrap a Lex'd matrix back to a plain `Fin n ‚Üí Fin n ‚Üí Nat`. | Definition |
| `ofMatrixLex_toMatrixLex` | 3266-3267 | `ofMatrixLex (toMatrixLex M) = M`. | `@[simp]` |
| `toMatrixLex_ofMatrixLex` | 3269-3270 | `toMatrixLex (ofMatrixLex M) = M`. | `@[simp]` |
| `canonFormImages` | 3278-3287 | The Finset of Lex-wrapped `canonAdj` images over all `DirAssignment`s for a leaf chain ‚ÄĒ the candidate set `canonForm` minimises over. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `canonForm` | 3297-3317 | **The canonical leaf adjacency matrix:** the lex-min `canonAdj` over all `DirAssignment`s (row-major lex). Requires `Nonempty (DirAssignment P‚āÄ chain.D)`. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `canonForm_mem_image` | 3319-3334 | **`canonForm` comes from some `DirAssignment`:** it equals `canonAdj ŌÉ` for some `ŌÉ`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `canonForm_le_canonAdj` | 3336-3352 | **`canonForm` is the lex-minimum:** `toMatrixLex (canonForm) ‚Č§ toMatrixLex (canonAdj ŌÉ)` for every `DirAssignment ŌÉ`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `LinearOracleSpec` | 3356-3372 | **The linear-oracle interface type:** given a leaf chain and a current-branch `DirAssignment`, return either `none` or a verified automorphism of `adj` (bundled as a subtype). | Definition |
| `some_isAut` | 3379-3391 | **Soundness (subtype-level):** when the oracle returns `some result`, the returned permutation is automatically an automorphism. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `LeafTwistSpec` | 3393-3410 | **Leaf-twist validity spec:** when the oracle returns `some result`, the returned `ŌÄ` relabels the input branch's canonical adjacency to that of some other `DirAssignment ŌÉ'` ‚ÄĒ the property justifying pruning. | Definition |
| `individualizedColouring` | 3448-3452 | **Fresh-colour individualisation** of a vertex set `S`: each `v ‚ąą S` gets unique colour `v.val + 1`; vertices outside `S` share colour `0`. | Definition |
| `FixesPointwise` | 3454-3457 | Predicate: permutation `ŌÄ` fixes every vertex in `S` pointwise (`ŌÄ v = v` for `v ‚ąą S`). | Definition |
| `complement` | 3463-3471 | A pointwise-fixing permutation stabilises the complement setwise: `v ‚ąČ S` implies `ŌÄ v ‚ąČ S`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `individualizedColouring_invariant` | 3475-3484 | An automorphism fixing `S` pointwise preserves the individualised colouring: `Ōá_S (ŌÄ v) = Ōá_S v` for every `v`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `warmRefine_invariant_of_isAut` | 3560-3569 | Warm refinement preserves automorphism invariance: if `(adj, P, Ōá_init)` are all `ŌÄ`-invariant, so is `warmRefine adj P Ōá_init`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `signature_transport` | 3583-3608 | **Signature transport.** An automorphism `g` carrying `(P‚āĀ, Ōá‚āĀ)` to `(P‚āā, Ōá‚āā)` maps the `(P‚āā, Ōá‚āā)`-signature at `g v` to the `(P‚āĀ, Ōá‚āĀ)`-signature at `v`. Cross-config form of `signature_invariant_of_isAut`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `sigKey_transport` | 3610-3617 | **`sigKey` transport** ‚ÄĒ cross-config: `sigKey adj P‚āā Ōá‚āā (g v) = sigKey adj P‚āĀ Ōá‚āĀ v`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `refineStep_transport` | 3619-3627 | **`refineStep` transport** ‚ÄĒ one round, cross-config: `refineStep adj P‚āā Ōá‚āā (g v) = refineStep adj P‚āĀ Ōá‚āĀ v`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `iterate_refineStep_transport` | 3629-3643 | **Iterated `refineStep` transport** across any number of rounds, cross-config. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `warmRefine_transport` | 3645-3654 | **Warm-refinement transport.** An automorphism carrying `(P‚āĀ, Ōá‚āĀ)` to `(P‚āā, Ōá‚āā)` carries the warm refinement of the first onto the second. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `OrbitPartition` | 3670-3676 | **Aut_S orbit relation** on vertices: `v ~ w` iff some automorphism of `adj` preserving `P` and fixing `S` pointwise sends `v` to `w`. | Definition |
| `refl` | 3682-3685 | Reflexivity of `OrbitPartition` (via the identity permutation). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `symm` | 3687-3702 | Symmetry of `OrbitPartition` (via permutation inverse). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `trans` | 3704-3719 | Transitivity of `OrbitPartition` (via permutation composition). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `subset_warmRefine` | 3721-3736 | **Trivial direction of the squeeze:** orbits refine 1-WL cells ‚ÄĒ `OrbitPartition v w` implies `warmRefine` colours of `v` and `w` agree. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `refineStep_iter_le_eq` | 3749-3767 | Refinement is split-only across iterations: equality at iterate `k + d` implies equality at iterate `k`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `warmRefine_eq_iter_eq` | 3769-3783 | `warmRefine` equality implies iterate-`r` equality for any `r ‚Č§ n`; the bridge from the fixpoint partition to any earlier-round partition. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `id_of_discrete_invariant` | 3808-3817 | **Fact B (pointwise):** a `ŌÄ`-invariant discrete colouring forces `ŌÄ` to be the identity. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `aut_trivial_of_discrete_warmRefine` | 3819-3835 | **Fact B (CFI):** if `warmRefine adj P Ōá_S` is discrete, every automorphism preserving `(adj, P)` and fixing `S` pointwise is the identity. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `orbit_iff_eq_of_discrete_warmRefine` | 3837-3855 | **Fact B (partition):** at discrete depth, `OrbitPartition adj P S v w ‚ÜĒ v = w`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `CascadesAt` | 3877-3884 | **Cascade-at-depth-`k` predicate:** some `S` with `S.card ‚Č§ k` makes `warmRefine adj P (individualizedColouring n S)` discrete. | Definition |
| `cascadesAt_univ` | 3886-3905 | **Trivial cascade at depth `n`:** taking `S = univ` gives a discrete starting colouring preserved by warm refinement ‚ÄĒ the every-graph fallback. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `theorem_1_HOR_at_depth` | 3925-3948 | **Key theorem (Tier 1 HOR).** If `adj` cascades at depth `k`, some `S` with `S.card ‚Č§ k` makes `warmRefine` discrete and the `Aut_S`-orbit partition equal to the `warmRefine` partition. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `theorem_1_HOR_at_n` | 3970-3981 | **Theorem 1, trivial-bound corollary:** every graph admits orbit recovery at depth `n`. Axiom-free specialisation to `cascadesAt_univ`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `theorem_1_HOR` | 3983-3994 | **Theorem 1 (legacy existential form):** some `S` makes `warmRefine` discrete and orbits equal cells. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `theorem_1_HOR_pointwise` | 3996-4008 | **Theorem 1, pointwise corollary:** at the cascade depth, every automorphism preserving `(adj, P)` and fixing `S` is the identity. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `SchemeProfile` | 4061-4077 | **Key structure (Tier 2).** Bundles a v-profile colouring with its structural facts: profile classes equal `Aut_v` orbits (schurian Step 1) and 1-WL refines the profile partition (intersection-number Step 2). | Structure |
| `warm_iff_profile` | 4083-4096 | **Squeeze for `SchemeProfile`:** the 1-WL fixpoint partition equals the profile partition. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `theorem_2_HOR_of_profile` | 4112-4128 | **Theorem 2 (assembly form):** given a `SchemeProfile` witness at `v`, the 1-WL fixpoint partition at depth 1 equals the `Aut_v`-orbit partition. The axiom-free assembly lemma `Scheme.lean`'s `theorem_2_HOR_concrete` consumes (the placeholder axioms `IsSchurianSchemeGraph` / `schurian_scheme_profile_exists` and the conditional `theorem_2_HOR` were retired 2026-06-05). | ‚ÄĒ |

| `CFIBase` | 57-68 | ¬ß1 A **CFI base graph** on `Fin m`: a simple (symmetric, loopless) `AdjMatrix m` with every vertex of degree at least 2 ‚ÄĒ the structural prerequisite for building CFI gadgets. | Structure |

| `IsCFI'.adj_symm` | 2103-2107 | ¬ß13.16.5 CFI adjacency is symmetric at the `Fin n` level: `adj.adj i j = adj.adj j i`. | ‚ÄĒ |

| `cfi_cascades_polynomially_oddDeg` | 2971-3175 | ¬ß13.24 M4 ‚ÄĒ for OddDegree CFI graphs, `warmRefine adj P Ōá_{allSeeds}` is `Discrete`; discharges `CascadesAt` (the cascade axiom) axiom-free at depth `cfi_depth_bound h`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `theorem_1_HOR_cfi_oddDeg` | 3177-3196 | **Tier-1 CFI orbit recovery.** Theorem 1 for OddDegree CFI graphs, axiom-free: orbit partition coincides with the warm-refined colouring at depth ‚Č§ baseSize, conditional only on `OddDegree`. | ‚ÄĒ |

**¬ß15 ‚ÄĒ Stage 3: gadget-flip automorphisms (the `Z‚āā^ő≤` generators).** *We build the generator
*existence* (the cycle-space flips), not the full `Aut(CFI) ‚ČÖ Z‚āā^ő≤ ‚čä Aut(H)` iso ‚ÄĒ the hard
surjectivity half is needed by no consumer. Both consumers (`LinearOracle.configSwap_of_aut`
and Tier-3a B1's `hwit`) want the same object: a CFI automorphism with controlled support,
realised by the even-subgraph (cycle-space) flip. Phases 0‚Äď1 below; Phases 2‚Äď6 (adjacency
preservation, `Fin n` lift, support/locality, `P`-preservation, consumer wiring) follow.*

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `card_symmDiff_mod_two` | **Parity helper.** `|S ‚ąÜ T| ‚Č° |S| + |T| (mod 2)` ‚ÄĒ the fact behind "an even subgraph preserves the even-subset invariant." | private |
| `CFIBase.flipSet` | The `F`-incident neighbours of `v` (`F : Fin m ‚Üí Fin m ‚Üí Bool` an even subgraph), as a subset of `N(v)`. | Definition |
| `CFIBase.symmDiff_flipSet_mem_even` | **Even-subset invariant preserved.** If every `flipSet F v` is even (`F` an even subgraph), `S ‚ąÜ flipSet F v` stays an even subset of `N(v)`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `CFIBase.cfiFlip` | **The cycle-space gadget flip** on `CFIVertex H`: toggles endpoint parities along `F` (`e^b_{v‚Üíw} ‚Ü¶ e^{b‚äēF v w}_{v‚Üíw}`) and complements subsets (`a_S^v ‚Ü¶ a_{S ‚ąÜ flipSet F v}^v`). | Definition (Phase 1) |
| `CFIBase.cfiFlip_involutive` | The gadget flip is an involution (`(S ‚ąÜ F) ‚ąÜ F = S`; `(b‚äēc)‚äēc = b`). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `CFIBase.cfiFlipEquiv` | The gadget flip as an `Equiv.Perm CFIVertex` (self-inverse). | Definition |
| `xor_eq_xor_iff` / `xor_ne_xor_iff` | Xor right-cancellation on `Bool` (`(a‚äēc) = (b‚äēc) ‚ÜĒ a = b`, and the `‚Č†` form). | private |
| `CFIBase.decide_mem_symmDiff_flipSet` | **Phase 2 bridge.** For `w ‚ąą N(v)`, `w ‚ąą S ‚ąÜ flipSet F v ‚ÜĒ (w‚ąąS) ‚äē F v w` ‚ÄĒ endpoint parity and subset membership flip together. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `CFIBase.cfiFlip_isAut` | **Phase 2 (the automorphism core).** For `F` an even subgraph that is symmetric (`F v w = F w v`), `cfiFlip F` preserves `cfiAdj` on every pair. Subset‚Äďendpoint: the `(w‚ąąS)‚äēb` invariant survives the joint flip; endpoint‚Äďendpoint bridge: the single edge `{v,w}` has one `F`-bit (symmetry), so `b‚āĀ=b‚āā` survives. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `IsCFI'.cfiFlipAut` | **Phase 3.** The gadget flip transported to `adj`'s vertices `Fin n` via the CFI labelling `h.e`: `g = e‚ĀĽ¬Ļ ‚ąė cfiFlip F ‚ąė e`. | Definition |
| `IsCFI'.e_cfiFlipAut` | Transport identity `e (g v) = cfiFlip F (e v)` ‚ÄĒ `e` intertwines the `Fin n` and `CFIVertex` flips. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `IsCFI'.isAut_cfiFlipAut` | **Phase-3 deliverable.** For `F` an even symmetric subgraph, `cfiFlipAut F ‚ąą Aut(adj)` ‚ÄĒ an honest `IsAut ‚Ä¶ adj` (via `matching` + `cfiFlip_isAut`) the consumers (`configSwap_of_aut`, Tier-3a `hwit`) use. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `IsCFI'.cfiFlipAut_involutive` | The lifted flip is an involution (needed where the decision pair must be *swapped*, `g a = b ‚ąß g b = a`). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `CFIBase.gadget` | **Phase 4.** The base vertex (gadget) of a CFI vertex. | Definition |
| `CFIBase.cfiFlip_eq_self_of_flipSet_empty` | **Locality.** If `F` has no edge at `x`'s gadget (`flipSet F (gadget x) = ‚ąÖ`), the flip fixes `x` (`S ‚ąÜ ‚ąÖ = S`; empty flip set ‚üĻ `F v w = false` ‚üĻ parity unchanged). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `IsCFI'.cfiFlipAut_eq_self_of_flipSet_empty` | Locality lifted to `Fin n`: `F` avoiding `i`'s gadget ‚üĻ `cfiFlipAut F` fixes `i`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `IsCFI'.disjoint_support_cfiFlipAut` | **Phase-4 deliverable.** If every vertex of a committed set `T` lives in an `F`-free gadget, then `Disjoint T (cfiFlipAut F).support` ‚ÄĒ the exact `Disjoint (committed set) ŌÄ.support` the path-fixing consumers (`hwit`, `configSwap`) require. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `CFIBase.cfiFlip_endpoint` / `_swap` | **C1b.0 recon.** The flip toggles `e^b_{v‚Üíw}`'s parity by `F v w`; so it swaps the parity-pair `e^0/e^1` iff `{v,w} ‚ąą F` ‚ÄĒ the primary flippable decision pair. | simp / ‚ÄĒ |
| `CFIBase.cfiFlip_subset` | The flip symmetric-differences `a_S^v` by `flipSet F v` ‚ÄĒ swaps the subset-pair iff the gadget is `F`-touched (the second flippable kind). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `IsCFI'.cfiFlipAut_endpointVertex` / `_swaps_endpointVertex` | **C1b.0 (lifted).** The `Fin n` swap fact: `cfiFlipAut F` swaps `endpointVertex hw false ‚ÜĒ true` iff `F v w = true` ‚ÄĒ the foundational swap C1b.1 keys on. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `triFlip_swaps_edge_01` | C1b.0 prototype validation: the triangle flip swaps the parity-pair on edge `{0,1}` (`decide`, independent confirmation). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `CFIBase.isEdgeOf` / `triEdge` | **C1b.2a.** The triangle even-subgraph through edge `{v,w}` with apex `u` ‚ÄĒ the minimal even subgraph through an edge. | Definition |
| `CFIBase.triEdge_eq_true` / `_iff` / `_symm` / `_cyclic` / `_apex` | Characterisation (membership, source-grouped), symmetry, cyclic invariance `{v,w,u}={w,u,v}`, and `F v w = true`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `CFIBase.flipSet_triEdge` / `_other` | The triangle's flip set is `{w,u}` at base vertex `v` (degree 2), and `‚ąÖ` off `{v,w,u}` (the avoidance ‚Üí D-locality). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `CFIBase.triEdge_even` | The triangle is an even subgraph (every vertex F-degree 2 or 0). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `CFIBase.exists_even_triangle` | **C1b.2a deliverable.** If the decision edge has a common neighbour `u` (distinct, in `N(v)‚ą©N(w)`), an even symmetric `F` through `{v,w}` exists with support `{v,w,u}` (avoids everything else) ‚ÄĒ the concrete cycle `F` cascade-1b needs, for triangle-containing bases. General triangle-free bases (K‚āÉ,‚āÉ, Petersen) need C1b.2b. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `CFIBase.evenPermEdge` | **C1b.2b.** The even-subgraph indicator of a permutation-cycle `ŌÉ` (the cycle's "next-vertex" map). A vertex's F-neighbours are `{ŌÉ p, ŌÉ‚ĀĽ¬Ļ p}` ‚ÄĒ degree 2, no list arithmetic. | Definition |
| `CFIBase.evenPermEdge_eq_true` / `_symm` / `_iff_of_mem` | Membership characterisation, symmetry, and the moved-vertex F-neighbours `= {ŌÉ p, ŌÉ‚ĀĽ¬Ļ p}`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `CFIBase.flipSet_evenPermEdge_of_mem` / `_of_fixed` | Flip set `= {ŌÉ p, ŌÉ‚ĀĽ¬Ļ p}` at a moved vertex (degree 2), `‚ąÖ` at a fixed point (avoidance). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `CFIBase.evenPermEdge_even` | The permutation-cycle is an even subgraph (degree 2 on the cycle via no-2-cycle, 0 off it). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `CFIBase.exists_even_cycle` | **C1b.2b deliverable.** A permutation-cycle `ŌÉ` through `{v,w}` (`ŌÉ v = w`) with H-edges (`hEdge`) and orbits ‚Č• 3 (`hNo2`) yields an even symmetric `F` through `{v,w}` avoiding every `ŌÉ`-fixed vertex. Subsumes the triangle; covers triangle-free bases. The cycle's *existence* in `H ‚ąí ő£` is the isolated graph hypothesis (where treewidth enters). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `IsCFI'.cfiFlipAut_preserves_P` | **Phase 5.** The gadget flip preserves any `P` that *every* `adj`-automorphism preserves (the descent's profile/trivial `P`) ‚ÄĒ transported through `isAut_cfiFlipAut`. Honest scope: a component-moving flip preserves exactly the automorphism-invariant `P`'s. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `IsCFI'.cfiFlipAut_pathFixing_witness` | **Phase-5 deliverable (Tier-3a B1 `hwit` shape).** Assembles Phases 3‚Äď5 + `g v = w` into `‚ąÉ ŌÄ, IsAut ŌÄ adj ‚ąß (‚ąÄ x u, P (ŌÄ x)(ŌÄ u) = P x u) ‚ąß Disjoint T ŌÄ.support ‚ąß ŌÄ v = w` ‚ÄĒ exactly what `Cascade.cascadeComposition_pathFixing`'s `hwit` consumes. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `triFlipEdges` / `triFlip_even` | **Phase-0 prototype:** `triangleBase`'s unique nontrivial even subgraph (all 3 edges; ő≤=1) and its even-flip-set fact. | Definition / ‚ÄĒ |

| `triFlip_isAut_check` | **Phase-0 crux:** the triangle gadget flip preserves `cfiAdj` on all 18√ó18 pairs (`decide`) ‚ÄĒ validates cycle-flip-is-automorphism on the smallest case before the general Phase-2 proof. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `triFlip_nontrivial` | Phase-0 smoke test: the triangle gadget flip moves some vertex ‚ÄĒ a nontrivial `CFI(triangle)` automorphism. | ‚ÄĒ |

| `CFIBase.mem_flipSet` | 3262-3265 | Membership in the flip set: `w ‚ąą flipSet F v ‚ÜĒ w ‚ąą N(v) ‚ąß F v w`. | `@[simp]` |
| `CFIBase.xorF` | 3293-3295 | **(CFI-cov.2)** Pointwise XOR of two flip-edge indicators ‚ÄĒ the cycle-space `Z‚āā` sum. | Definition |
| `CFIBase.flipSet_xorF` | 3297-3305 | **(CFI-cov.2)** The flip-set of an XOR is the symmetric difference of the flip-sets: `flipSet (xorF F F') v = flipSet F v ‚ąÜ flipSet F' v`. The reusable core of the cycle-space sum. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `CFIBase.even_xorF` | 3307-3314 | **(CFI-cov.2)** Even flip-subgraphs stay even under `xorF` (symmetric-difference preserves even cardinality, via `card_symmDiff_mod_two`). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `CFIBase.CycleSpace` | 3316-3319 | **(CFI-cov.2) The cycle space `Z‚āā^ő≤`**: symmetric, even flip-subgraphs `F` ‚ÄĒ the index set of the gauge flips `cfiFlip F` (the `Z‚āā^ő≤` factor of `Aut(CFI(H))`). | Definition |
| `CFIBase.cycleSpace_xorF` | 3321-3324 | **(CFI-cov.2)** The cycle space is closed under the `Z‚āā` sum `xorF` (symmetric + even both preserved). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `CFIBase.cycleSpace_const_false` | 3326-3330 | **(CFI-cov.2)** The empty flip-subgraph (zero) lies in the cycle space. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `CFIBase.cfiFlip_endpoint_swap` | 3451-3460 | **C1b.0.** The flip swaps the parity-pair `e^0_{v‚Üíw}/e^1_{v‚Üíw}` iff `F v w = true` (the swap companion of `cfiFlip_endpoint`). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `CFIBase.cfiFlip_xorF` | 3478-3493 | **(CFI-cov.3) Gauge flip is a homomorphism on the cycle space:** `cfiFlip (xorF F F') = cfiFlip F ‚ąė cfiFlip F'` (endpoint: Bool-xor assoc/comm; subset: symmDiff assoc/comm via `flipSet_xorF`). The `Z‚āā^ő≤`-factor group structure. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `CFIBase.cfiFlip_const_false` | 3495-3506 | **(CFI-cov.3)** The zero subgraph is the identity flip: `cfiFlip (fun _ _ => false) = id` (cycle-space zero ‚Ü¶ identity). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `CFIBase.flipSet_triEdge_other` | 3568-3578 | **D-locality.** Off the triangle `{v,w,u}` the triangle's flip set is empty, so the triangle flip fixes every other gadget. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `CFIBase.flipSet_evenPermEdge_of_fixed` | 3664-3673 | **D-locality (triangle-free bases).** At a `ŌÉ`-fixed vertex the permutation-cycle flip set is empty, so the cycle flip avoids every fixed gadget. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `IsCFI'.cfiFlipAut_swaps_endpointVertex` | 3837-3849 | **C1b.0 (lifted to `Fin n`).** `cfiFlipAut F` swaps `endpointVertex hw false ‚ÜĒ true` iff `F v w = true` ‚ÄĒ the foundational decision-pair swap C1b.1 keys on. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `IsCFI'.cfiFlipAut_xorF` | 3853-3861 | **(CFI-cov.3) The lifted gauge-flip homomorphism:** `cfiFlipAut (xorF F F') = cfiFlipAut F * cfiFlipAut F'` (the `Fin n` form of `cfiFlip_xorF` via `e_cfiFlipAut`). So `F ‚Ü¶ cfiFlipAut F` is a group homomorphism `(Z‚āā^ő≤, xorF) ‚Üí Equiv.Perm (Fin n)`, image the gauge group. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `IsCFI'.cfiFlipAut_one` | 3863-3869 | **(CFI-cov.3)** The zero gauge flip is the identity: `cfiFlipAut (fun _ _ => false) = 1` ‚ÄĒ the homomorphism preserves the unit. | ‚ÄĒ |

| `AssociationScheme` | 47-91 | A symmetric association scheme on `Fin n`: a partition of `Fin n √ó Fin n` into `rank + 1` symmetric relations `R_0, ‚Ä¶, R_rank` (`R_0` the diagonal) with well-defined intersection numbers `p^k_{ij}`. | Structure |
| `relOfPair` | 107-109 | ¬ß1.1 The unique relation index `i : Fin (S.rank + 1)` for which `rel i v w = true`. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `rel_relOfPair` | 111-114 | The pair `(v, w)` lies in `R_{relOfPair v w}`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `relOfPair_unique` | 116-119 | Uniqueness: any relation containing `(v, w)` is `relOfPair v w`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `rel_iff_relOfPair` | 121-124 | Characterisation: `rel i v w = true ‚ÜĒ i = relOfPair v w`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `relOfPair_symm` | 126-131 | `relOfPair v w = relOfPair w v`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `relOfPair_eq_zero_iff` | 139-147 | Diagonal characterisation: `relOfPair v w = 0 ‚ÜĒ v = w`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `AssociationScheme.ClosedSubset` | 161-166 | **(EOL scheme leg) Closed relation subset = block system.** `I` contains the diagonal `R_0` and is closed under the complex product (`R_i,R_j ‚ąą I` and `intersectionNumber i j k ‚Č† 0` ‚üĻ `R_k ‚ąą I`). The association-scheme form of a block system / sub-equivalence; on a schurian scheme graph it is a union of scheme relations, hence refinement-visible. | Definition |
| `AssociationScheme.schemeEquiv` | 168-171 | **(EOL scheme leg) The equivalence induced by a relation subset:** `v ~ w` iff `relOfPair v w ‚ąą I`. Under `ClosedSubset` it is a genuine equivalence (the block system). | Definition |
| `AssociationScheme.schemeEquiv_trans` | 181-198 | **Transitivity from closure under the complex product.** `w` witnesses `intersectionNumber (relOfPair v w)(relOfPair w x)(relOfPair v x) ‚Č† 0`, so the `ClosedSubset` closure clause forces `relOfPair v x ‚ąą I`. Where the scheme's intersection numbers do the work a raw partition could not. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `AssociationScheme.closedSubset_univ` | 205-207 | The whole relation set is always closed (the trivial "one block" system). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `AssociationScheme.IsPrimitive` | 209-214 | **(EOL scheme leg) Scheme primitivity:** the only closed subsets are the diagonal `{R_0}` and the whole relation set ‚ÄĒ no non-trivial block system. The Cameron-free, scheme-theoretic primitivity for the Exhaustive-Obstruction Lemma's leg C on coherent-configuration residuals. | Definition |
| `AssociationScheme.exists_nontrivial_closedSubset_of_not_isPrimitive` | 216-225 | **(Imprimitive ‚üĻ non-trivial block system)** Unfolding `¬¨IsPrimitive`: there is a closed subset `I` neither `{R_0}` nor `univ` ‚ÄĒ a genuine non-trivial block system. The entry point letting the Route B imprimitive discharge construct its partition `ő≤` (the `schemeEquiv I` block-class) from the descent's combinatorial `¬¨IsPrimitive` observation. Via `push Not`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `AssociationScheme.schemeEquiv_class_eq_iff` | 227-245 | **(Block-class equality characterization)** `{y | schemeEquiv I u y} = {y | schemeEquiv I w y} ‚ÜĒ schemeEquiv I u w` for a closed subset `I` ‚ÄĒ the `schemeEquiv I`-classes are the blocks, equal iff their basepoints are related. The honest characterization of the Route B partition `ő≤ v := {y | schemeEquiv I v y}`, needed wherever `ő≤ u = ő≤ w` must be related back to the scheme (e.g. a future non-recovering `hfiber`). Standard equivalence-class machinery on `schemeEquiv_equivalence`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `AssociationScheme.exists_composable_of_intersectionNumber` | 247-265 | **(Phase 2, M1.1c ‚ÄĒ general)** A nonzero intersection number is realized by a composable triple: `R_k` nonempty ‚ąß `intersectionNumber i j k ‚Č† 0 ‚üĻ ‚ąÉ x y z, (x,y) ‚ąą R_i ‚ąß (y,z) ‚ąą R_j ‚ąß (x,z) ‚ąą R_k`. The general ingredient the `ClosedSubset`-closure clause needs (reusable for the ¬ß5.3 general crux: "the difference of a composite relation is the sum of the parts'"). `R_k`-nonemptiness explicit (the axioms do not force every index inhabited). | ‚ÄĒ |

## ChainDescent/CascadeOracle.lean

The a-priori cascade-oracle Lean contract (plan: `docs/Archive/ChainDescent/chain-descent-cascade-oracle-lean-brief.md`). Builds axiom-clean (only `refineStep`/`refineStep_iff` + Lean foundationals), no `sorry`. Phase A = soundness/validity, Phase B = the completeness reduction (wired to the axiom-free orbit-recovery theorems), Phase C = the residual obligations: verdict iso-invariance is *discharged conditionally* (`verdictIsoInvariant_of_complete` ‚ÄĒ it reduces to localisation), and localisation is *split* into (1a) bounded-depth recoverability ‚ÄĒ **proved** on the cascade class (`RecoverableByDepth` + `recoverableByDepth_cfi`/`_scheme`, anchored by `cellsAreOrbits_of_discrete`) ‚ÄĒ and (1b) intermediate-to-deep bridging, **open but not GI ‚ąą P** (cascade-class construction correctness). Only general-class completeness is the GI ‚ąą P obligation. ¬ßC.0 also proves the deferred-decisions foundation `real_stays_real`.

| Name | Line | Description | Notes |
|------|------|-------------|-------|
| `mono` | 59-68 | ¬ßC.0 Orbit monotonicity: an `Aut_{S'}`-orbit pair stays an orbit pair at every smaller individualized set `S ‚äÜ S'`, so a certified merge can be reused at shallower nodes. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `real_stays_real` | 70-78 | ¬ßC.0 Deferred-decisions foundation: a genuine decision (no orbit relation) at `S` is still genuine at every larger `S' ‚äá S`, so deferring a real decision never loses it. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `orbitPartition_of_support_disjoint` | 112-126 | ¬ßC.0.1 **Support backbone.** An automorphism that fixes the individualized set `S` pointwise and sends `v ‚Ü¶ w` certifies that `v, w` share an `Aut_S`-orbit. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `exists_orbit_witness_of_aut` | 128-138 | ¬ßC.0.1 **Availability depth.** A symmetry of support size `s` keeps its orbit pair certifiable down to individualized sets of size `n ‚ąí s` ‚ÄĒ full-support symmetries only at the root, transpositions almost to the leaves. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `CascadeOracleSpec` | 140-152 | The a-priori cascade-oracle interface: at an internal descent node, return either `none` or a verified automorphism merging two representatives. The cascade analogue of `LinearOracleSpec` (not leaf-gated). | Definition |
| `some_isAut` | 159-167 | **Soundness (subtype-level):** when the oracle returns `some result`, the returned permutation is automatically an automorphism. | ‚ÄĒ |

| `merged_sameCell` | 183-194 | A sound oracle only ever merges vertices that 1-WL already left in the same cell, so it never collapses across cells. | ‚ÄĒ |
