| `pencilDisc_eval` | 159-166 | Evaluating `pencilDisc A B` at `(y, z)` recovers `det(y¬∑A + z¬∑B)`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `polar_pencil` | 171-176 | Polar of the pencil form `y‚ÄĘP + z‚ÄĘR` is the linear combination of the polars. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `polarRad_eq_bot_iff_separatingRight` | 178-188 | The polar-radical is trivial ‚üļ the polar bilinear form separates on the right. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `polarRad_ne_bot_iff_det_eq_zero` | 190-195 | **Degeneracy ‚üļ vanishing determinant** (the bridge linchpin). For a basis `b`, the pencil member `G` is degenerate (`polarRad G ‚Č† ‚ä•`) iff the determinant of the Gram matrix of its polar form vanishes. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `toMatrix‚āā_polarBilin_pencil` | 197-207 | In matrix coordinates, the pencil `y‚ÄĘP + z‚ÄĘR`'s polar bilinear form is `y¬∑(matrix of P.polarBilin) + z¬∑(matrix of R.polarBilin)`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `pencilZeros_count_le` | 211-225 | The Schwartz‚ÄďZippel count over `K √ó K` (via the `(y,z) ‚Ü¶ ![y,z]` bijection). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `degenerate_count_le` | 227-259 | **The good-anchor degenerate-pencil count.** Given a good anchor, the number of degenerate pencil ratios `(y,z)` is `‚Č§ d¬∑(card K)` (Schwartz‚ÄďZippel on the pencil discriminant). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `sum_two_bucket_le` | 267-286 | **Two-bucket sum bound.** Split `s` by predicate `p`; if `g ‚Č§ Ma` on the `¬¨p` bucket and `g ‚Č§ Mb` on the `p` bucket, with cardinalities `‚Č§ Ca`, `‚Č§ Cb` respectively (and `Ma, Mb ‚Č• 0`), then `‚ąĎ_{i‚ąąs} g i ‚Č§ Ca¬∑Ma + Cb¬∑Mb`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `sqrt_mul_le_div` | 288-296 | **Deg-bucket magnitude.** If `r¬∑k ‚Č§ V` (the proper-subspace radical bound), then `‚ąö(V¬∑r) ‚Č§ V/‚ąök`. Used with `r = |radical F_{y,z}|`, `k = |K|`, `V = card V`: a degenerate member contributes at most `card V / ‚ąö|K|`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `c0_le` | 298-334 | **The final c‚āÄ bound (3e-iii finish).** From the counting bound `2¬∑NS ‚Č§ 2¬∑z_u + n + T` (`card_agree_le`), the `|T|` bound `T ‚Č§ q¬∑‚ąön + d¬∑n/‚ąöq` (`normT_bucket_bound`, √∑q), and the zero-count `z_u¬∑q ‚Č§ n + (q‚ąí1)¬∑n/‚ąöq` (`zeroCount_sq_le` with the proper-subspace radical bound), under the threshold‚Ä¶ | ‚ÄĒ |
| `norm_quadraticChar` | 342-356 | The quadratic character composed into `‚Ąā` has norm `0` at `0` and `1` elsewhere. | ‚ÄĒ |

## ChainDescent/ScratchSimilitudeCap.lean

**Viability spike (2026-06-29), NOT in `build.sh`** ‚ÄĒ the "similitude cap" closing the last in-architecture-poly lead.
Formalizes that the affine-polar graph determines `Q` only up to scaling (a similitude), so refinement is provably
capped at the **square class**: `Ōá(det G‚āā)` is a graph invariant, but the exact form value (and the singleton square
class) is not. Verdict consequence: the `Ōá(det G‚āā)` refinement route is provably quasipoly, not poly ‚ÄĒ the dividing
line for poly is *coloring vs group* (Route C / `CellsAreOrbits`), not square-class vs field-value. Axiom-clean
`[propext, Classical.choice, Quot.sound]`, builds on `PairForm`.

| Name | Line | Description | Notes |
|------|------|-------------|-------|
| `quad_smul_apply` | 49-51 | Scaling the form scales its values: `(c ‚ÄĘ Q) x = c * Q x`. | `@[simp]` |
| `polar_smul` | 54-55 | Scaling the form scales its polar: `polar (c ‚ÄĘ Q) s a = c * polar Q s a`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `adj_smul_iff` | 59-61 | **The similitude cap (T1).** The affine-polar adjacency `Q x = 0` is unchanged by scaling the form (`c ‚Č† 0`). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `affinePolarAdj_smul_eq` | 65-68 | **The graph is identical for `Q` and `c‚ÄĘQ`.** The adjacency relation `(x,y) ‚Ü¶ Q(x‚ąíy)=0` is *literally equal*, so the graph determines `Q` only up to scaling ‚ÄĒ any isomorphism-invariant of a vertex pair must be invariant under `Q ‚Ü¶ c‚ÄĘQ`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `pairForm_smul_apply` | 71-75 | The pair invariant scales by `c¬≤`: `pairForm (c‚ÄĘQ) a s = c¬≤ ¬∑ pairForm Q a s`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `chi_sq_mul` | 78-87 | `Ōá(c¬≤ ¬∑ v) = Ōá(v)` for `c ‚Č† 0` ‚ÄĒ the square multiplier is invisible to the quadratic character. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `chi_pairForm_smul` | 90-92 | **The square class is a graph invariant (T2).** `Ōá(det G‚āā) = Ōá(pairForm)` is unchanged by scaling the form (`c¬≤` killed by `Ōá`) ‚ÄĒ why the canonizer's pair observable is well-defined on the graph (= on the scaling class of `Q`). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `chi_singleton_smul` | 97-99 | **The singleton square class is NOT a graph invariant (T3a).** `Ōá((c‚ÄĘQ) a) = Ōá(c)¬∑Ōá(Q a)` flips by `Ōá(c)` ‚ÄĒ the formal proof of the empirical "singleton `Z_u({t})` is binary" finding (only the `Ōá(c)`-invariant fact `Q=0` survives). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `pairForm_value_not_invariant` | 104-106 | **The exact value is NOT a graph invariant (T3b).** The exact pair value scales by `c¬≤`, so presentations `Q`, `c‚ÄĘQ` of the *same graph* disagree on it whenever `c¬≤ ‚Č† 1` ‚ÄĒ no isomorphism-invariant procedure (refinement of any dimension, or Route C) recovers the exact form value, only its square class. | ‚ÄĒ |

## ChainDescent/ScratchOrbitBaseCase.lean

**CellsAreOrbits route, increment 1 + 2 (2026-06-29), NOT in `build.sh`.** The base case of the `CellsAreOrbits`
induction (the open core of the forms-graph poly route) + the multiplier-rigidity delimiter + the free-prefix orbit
coarsening. Models affine-polar automorphisms as `Similitude Q` (`g : V ‚ČÉ‚āó V`, `őľ ‚Č† 0`, `Q‚ąėg = őľ¬∑Q`). Axiom-clean
`[propext, Classical.choice, Quot.sound]`, pure geometry (no `Fintype`). Builds on `PairForm`. See
`docs/chain-descent-cellsareorbits-route.md`.

| Name | Line | Description | Notes |
|------|------|-------------|-------|
| `Similitude` | 44-48 | A similitude of `Q`: a linear equiv `g` with `Q (g x) = mult ¬∑ Q x`, `mult ‚Č† 0`. An isometry is `mult = 1`. | Structure |
| `affinePolar_empty_base_one_orbit` | 52-53 | **Depth 0** ‚ÄĒ the whole vertex set is one orbit (translations): `‚ąÄ v w, ‚ąÉ t, v + t = w`. `CellsAreOrbits` at `S = ‚ąÖ`, free. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `mult_eq_one_of_fixes_anisotropic` | 58-63 | **The delimiter.** A similitude fixing an anisotropic vector (`Q v ‚Č† 0`) has `mult = 1`. Once an anisotropic vector is pinned, residual similitudes are isometries. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `mult_eq_one_of_fixes_span_anisotropic` | 68-77 | Delimiter, span form: fixing a set whose span contains an anisotropic vector forces `mult = 1` ‚ÄĒ so multiplier freedom in `Stab(S)` requires `span S` totally isotropic. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `WittConeTransitive` | 81-83 | **Isolated Witt input**: isometries act transitively on nonzero isotropic vectors. Discharged (mod the residual) in `ScratchWittCone`. | Definition |
| `neighborSphere_zero_eq_isotropic` | 87-88 | The graph-neighbours of `0` are exactly the nonzero isotropic vectors (`Q(v‚ąí0)=0 ‚üļ Q v = 0`). | ‚ÄĒ |
| `depth1_isotropic_sphere_one_orbit` | 93-97 | **Depth 1** ‚ÄĒ the isotropic neighbour sphere is one isometry-orbit, given `WittConeTransitive`. The second base rung. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `scalarEquiv` / `scalarEquiv_apply` | 109-119 | The scalar automorphism `x ‚Ü¶ l ‚ÄĘ x` (`l ‚Č† 0`) as a linear equiv, and its apply lemma. | Def / `@[simp]` |
| `scalarSimilitude` | 121-126 | The scalar similitude `x ‚Ü¶ l ‚ÄĘ x`, multiplier `l¬≤`, fixing the origin ‚ÄĒ realizes every square multiplier in `Stab(0)` with no Witt input. | Definition |
| `StabOrbit` | 128-129 | The `Stab(S)`-orbit relation: `w'` reachable from `w` by a similitude fixing `S` pointwise. | Definition |
| `stabOrbit_preserves_norm_of_anisotropic_base` | 136-147 | **Wall side (orbit level).** At an anisotropic base, every `Stab(S)`-orbit preserves the exact norm `Q` (`mult = 1`) ‚ÄĒ orbits are norm-fine, strictly finer than square-class cells. The open core located at the orbit level. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `stabOrbit_zero_base_scales` | 149-168 | **Free side at the origin (no Witt).** `l ‚ÄĘ w` is in the `Stab({0})`-orbit of `w` with `Q(l‚ÄĘw) = l¬≤¬∑Q w` ‚ÄĒ origin-base orbits are square-class-coarse, matching refinement. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `TotallyIsotropic` | 170-171 | A base `S` is totally isotropic when `Q` vanishes on `span S`. | Definition |
| `MultiplierRealizable` | 175-179 | `Stab(S)` realizes every nonzero multiplier (the multiplier freedom the free prefix runs on). | Definition |
| `WittRealizes` | 181-183 | **Carried Witt-decomposition input (W-dec)**: over every totally-isotropic base, all multipliers are realizable. | Definition |
| `stabOrbit_realizable_base_scales` | 189-198 | **Increment 2** ‚ÄĒ free-prefix orbit coarsening: given `MultiplierRealizable Q S`, the `Stab(S)`-orbit of `w` reaches norm `őľ¬∑Q w` for every `őľ ‚Č† 0`. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `not_multiplierRealizable_of_anisotropic` | 200-210 | The delimiter at predicate level: `MultiplierRealizable Q S` fails once `S` carries an anisotropic vector (with a `őľ ‚Č† 0, 1` witness). The free/‚Äčwall boundary. | ‚ÄĒ |
| `stabOrbit_totallyIsotropic_scales` | 212-216 | **Increment 2 capstone** ‚ÄĒ free-prefix orbit coarsening over any totally-isotropic base, modulo the carried `WittRealizes`. | ‚ÄĒ |
